			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Chipotle ANNOUNCES </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">FIRST</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;"> QUARTER </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">2020</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;"> RESULTS</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Q1 COMPs grew 3.3%, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Digital Sales grew 80.8% and accounted for 26.3% of sales</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt solid #996633 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">

			<a name="_Hlk504391754"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">I am grateful to all our employees for their </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">commitment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and efforts in providing guests access to our safe, delicious, high-quality food made from real ingredients during this unprecedented time," said&nbsp;Brian Niccol, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chairman and CEO</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, Chipotle.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">"</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Investing in digital over the last several years has allowed us to quickly pivot our business with Q1 digital sales reaching our highest ever quarterly level of $372 million. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Our strong brand, business model and balance sheet give us the confidence to not only weather this downturn but continue to judiciously invest in key areas s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">o</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> that when we come out the other side, we will emerge even stronger."</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">COVID-19 and Liquidity Update:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle remains focused on the safety and well-being of our employees, guests, and our food as we navigate the challenges presented by COVID-19. We are dedicated to keeping our restaurants stocked with gloves, hand sanitizers, masks, and a tamper evident packaging seal for contactless mobile pickup and delivery orders. Our industry leading food safety protocols result in a culture of continuous improvement to ensure that our customers have consistently excellent experiences. In response to COVID-19, we quickly made critical decisions including: eliminated non-essential travel, implemented work from home, significantly expanded employee benefits, increased sanitization of high touch, high traffic areas, and increased the frequency of personal hygiene practices. All of these initiatives give our employees and customers confidence that Chipotle remains steadfast in our commitment </font>
		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

</div><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

		</p>

</div>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">to keeping them safe.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle has a strong financial position with $909.2 million in cash, restricted cash, and short-term investments as of March 31, 2020 and no debt. In addition, while the Company doesn&#x2019;t intend to utilize the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Paycheck Protection Program (PPP)</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> loan provision of the recently passed Coronavirus Aid, Relief, and Economic Security (CARES) Act, we expect to see a liquidity benefit of about $100 million primarily from deferring social security tax payments and accelerating tax depreciation in previous returns as allowed by the CARES Act.&nbsp; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">As sales fell quickly from the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">impact of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">COVID</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">-19</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, we proactively</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> implemented a number of actions</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">reduce</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> cash outlays and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">expenses, including the suspension of our stock buyback program</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> As a result of these efforts and our solid balance sheet as well as the added liquidity from CARES tax deferrals, we believe we have enough cash to sustain us for well over a year. However, if the recovery takes longer than expected, we have the ability to make additional adjustments as needed.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Results for the three months ended </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">March</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">: &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Revenue in the first quarter increased to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$1.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> billion, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">7.8%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> compared with the same quarter a year ago, driven by a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">3.3%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> increase in comparable restaurant sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> that includes a 1.3% benefit related to leap day</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. Comparable restaurant sales improved </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to a 4.9% increase in average check, which includes a 2.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% benefit from menu price increases that were implemented during 2019, partially offset by a 1.4% decrease in comparable restaurant transactions.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> Cadence of monthly comparable restaurant sales during the quarter was: January +12.1%, February +17.1% (including 4.3% benefit of leap day), and March -16.0%. Comparable restaurant sales troughed at -35.0% during the week ending March 29</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">th</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and have improved in April with the past week, adjusted for Easter, being down in the high teens. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">D</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">igital sales grew 8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0.8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% year over year to $37</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1.8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the Company&#x2019;s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> highest ever quarterly level, and represented 26.3% of sales. A</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">fter our dining rooms closed to help control the spread of COVID-19</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> moved swiftly by driving further investments towards digital and delivery designed to reduce friction while increasing convenient access.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> This included reprioritizing marketing efforts by offering free delivery from March 15 to at least early May, shifting media spend from live sports to more online and streaming platforms, and announcing a national delivery partnership with Uber Eats. As a result, digital sales for the month of March grew 102.6% year over year and represented 37.6% of sales.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">We opened 19 new restaurants including one relocation during the quarter and closed two restaurants, bringing the total restaurant count to 2,638. We have several restaurants set to open and another 49 under construction; however, we have begun to see construction delays and have preemptively delayed groundbreaking on the majority of projects in April.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Food, beverage and packaging costs were </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">32.8%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> of revenue, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">60</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> basis points compared to the first quarter of 2019.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">crease was primarily due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">food expenses related to Chipotle Rewards</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> higher costs of several ingredients, partially offset by the benefit of menu price increases in late 2019 and, to a lesser extent, lower paper costs.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was 17.6%, a decrease from 21.0% in the first quarter of 2019 driven primarily by wage inflation at the crew level, increased marketing and promotional spend, higher costs of several ingredients, and delivery expense associated with increased delivery sales, partially offset by leverage from the comparable restaurant sales increase. The sudden change to our business due to COVID-19 in March resulted in a short term, outsized impact to labor and food costs. Labor costs were elevated as we accommodated crew needs, shifted hours to support our growing digital business, and made additional employee investments in the form of extra assistance pay and elevated quarterly bonuses. Similarly, our food costs were elevated as we worked to right size food purchases to align with the new sales level.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">General and administrative expenses for the quarter were $106.5 million on a GAAP basis, or $99.8 million on a non-GAAP basis, excluding $5.2 million </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">for charges related primarily to the 2017 agreement with our former Executive Chairman Steve Ells</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and $1.4 million related to transformation expenses. GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> also include underlying general and administrative expenses totaling $77.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, $15.7 million related to non-cash stock compensation, $4.3 million related payroll taxes on stock option exercises, and $2.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million related to our All Manager Conference</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> that was moved to 2021 due to COVID-19.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The effective income tax rate for the three months ended March 31, 2020 was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">negative </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">3.4%, a dec</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">rease from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">an effective tax rate of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">22.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% for the three months ended March 31, 2019, primarily due to excess tax benefits </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">related to option exercises and equity vesting in the quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$76.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$2.70</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, a decrease from</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> $88.1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$3.13</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, in the first quarter of 2019. Excluding the impact of restaurant closure costs, certain other costs, and corporate restructuring adjusted net </font>
		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

		</p>

</div><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

		</p>

</div>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">income was $8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">7.2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and adjusted diluted earnings per share was $3.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">08</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle also announced today it has signed a Deferred Prosecution Agreement to resolve the previously disclosed investigation </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">conducted by the U.S. Attorney&#x2019;s Office for the Central District of California, in conjunction with the U.S. Food and Drug Administration&#x2019;s Office of Criminal Investigations related to past food safety incidents beginning in 2015. Pursuant to the Agreement, the government has agreed to take no action relating to these past incidents for three years provided that Chipotle complies with its obligations under the Agreement, which include paying a $25 million fine (consisting of a $10 million payment by June 1, 2020, followed by three separate payments of $5 million each to be paid every 30 days after the first payment) and enhancing and maintaining its existing comprehensive compliance program, which is designed to ensure that it complies with all applicable federal and state food safety laws. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">More information will be available in our Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q, which will be filed with the SEC by the end of April.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Outlook</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Given the level of volatility and uncertainty surrounding the future impact of COVID-19 on the broader US economy and any specific impact to our company, we are withdrawing our previous fiscal 2020 guidance related to comparable restaurant sales growth, new restaurant openings, and effective full year tax rate.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Definitions</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> following</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> definitions apply to these terms as used throughout this release:</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Comparable restaurant sales, or sales comps, and comparable restaurant transactions, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represent the change in period-over-period sales or transactions for restaurants in operation for at least 13 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Average restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">refer to the average trailing 12-month sales for restaurants in operation for at least 12 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Conference Call</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;"> Details</font>

		</p>

		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> 2,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">00 restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">March 31</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. With more than </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">85</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">,000 employees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the food industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. Steve Ells, founder and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">former </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">executive chairman, first opened Chipotle with a single restaurant in Denver, Colorado in 1993. For more information or to place an order online, visit</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Forward-Looking Statements </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Certain statements in this press release are forward-looking statements as defined in the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. We use words such as &#x201C;anticipate&#x201D;, &#x201C;believe&#x201D;, &#x201C;could&#x201D;, &#x201C;should&#x201D;, &#x201C;estimate&#x201D;, &#x201C;expect&#x201D;, &#x201C;intend&#x201D;, &#x201C;project&#x201D;, &#x201C;target&#x201D;, and similar terms and phrases, including references to assumptions, to identify forward-looking statements. The forward-looking statements in this press release are based on currently available operating, financial and competitive information available to us as of the date of this release and we assume no obligation to update these forward-looking statements. These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: the ongoing adverse effect of the novel coronavirus (COVID-19) pandemic on our guest traffic, restaurant sales and operating costs as a result of actions we have taken in response to the coronavirus, including closing some restaurants, ending dine in service at all restaurants while continuing to offer only takeout and/or delivery during modified work hours, extending enhanced benefits to employees impacted by the coronavirus, increasing compensation for restaurant employees, purchasing additional sanitation supplies and services and delaying the construction of new restaurant openings; risks that the impact of the coronavirus pandemic will continue for a long duration and may require a more drastic response, such as closing all or most restaurants; risks of food safety and food-borne illnesses and other health concerns about our food; risks associated with our reliance on certain information technology systems and potential failures or interruptions; privacy and cyber security risks related to our acceptance of electronic payments or electronic processing of confidential customer or employee information; the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the increasingly competitive labor market and our ability to attract and retain qualified employees; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due to our Food With Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased overall consumer spending (including but not limited to the increase in unemployment caused by the coronavirus pandemic), or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our increased focus on our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services, which are heightened during the pendency of government restrictions on dine in restaurant services as a result of the coronavirus pandemic; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions related to food safety incidents and potential class action litigation regarding employment laws, advertising claims or other matters; and other risk factors described from time to time in our SEC reports, including our annual report on Form 10-K and quarterly reports on Form 10-Q, all of which are available on the investor relations page of our website at ir.Chipotle.com.</font>

We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, and adjusted general and administrative expenses measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
